For classes that are either not found or are not supposed to\n    36→ * be loaded in isolation, this plugin classloader delegates their loading to its parent. This makes\n    37→ * this classloader a child-first classloader.\n    38→ * <p>\n    39→ * This class is thread-safe and parallel capable.\n    40→ */\n    41→public class PluginClassLoader extends for this plugin.\n    55→     * @param parent the parent classloader to be used for delegation for classes that were\n    56→     * not found or should not be loaded in isolation by this classloader.\n    57→     */\n    58→    public PluginClassLoader(URL pluginLocation, URL[] urls, ClassLoader parent) {\n    59→        super(urls, parent);\n    60→        this.pluginLocation = required by the plugin that\n    65→     * is loaded by this classloader.\n    66→     *\n    67→     * @return the plugin location.\n    68→     */\n    69→    public String location() {\n    70→        return pluginLocation.toString();\n    71→    }\n    72→\n    73→    @Override\n    74→    public String toString() {\n    75→        return \"PluginClassLoader{pluginLocation=\" + pluginLocation + \"}\";\n    76→    }\n    77→\n    78→    @Override\n    79→    public URL getResource(String name) {\n    80→        Objects.requireNonNull(name);\n    81→\n    82→        URL url = findResource(name);\n    83→        if (url == null) {\n    84→            url = super.getResource(name);\n    85→        }\n    86→        return url;\n    87→    }\n    88→\n    89→    @Override\n    90→    public Enumeration<URL> getResources(String name) throws IOException {\n    91→        Objects.requireNonNull(name);\n    92→        List<URL> resources = new ArrayList<>();\n    93→        for (Enumeration<URL> foundLocally = findResources(name); foundLocally.hasMoreElements();) {\n    94→            URL url = foundLocally.nextElement();\n    95→            if (url != null)\n    96→                resources.add(url);\n    97→        }\n    98→        // Explicitly call the parent implementation instead of super to avoid double-listing the local resources\n    99→        for (Enumeration<URL> foundByParent = getParent().getResources(name); foundByParent.hasMoreElements();) {\n   100→            URL url = foundByParent.nextElement();\n   101→            if (url != null)\n it is supposed to be called by multiple\n   108→    // Connect tasks. While findClass is thread-safe, defineClass called within loadClass of the\n   109→    // base method is not. More on multithreaded classloaders in:\n   110→    // https://docs.oracle.com/javase/7/docs/technotes/guides/lang/cl-mt.html\n   111→    @Override\n   112→    protected Class<?> loadClass(String name, boolean resolve) throws ClassNotFoundException {\n   113→        synchronized (getClassLoadingLock(name)) {\n   114→            Class<?> klass = findLoadedClass(name);\n   115→            if (klass == null) {\n   116→                try {\n   117→                    if (PluginUtils.shouldLoadInIsolation(name)) {\n   118→                        klass = findClass(name);\n   119→                    }\n   120→                } catch (ClassNotFoundException e) {\n   121→                    // Not found in loader's path. iterator::next);\n                } catch (ServiceConfigurationError t) {\n                    log.error(\"Failed to discover {} in {}{}\",\n                            type.simpleName(), source,       if (pluginKlass.getClassLoader() != source.loader()) {\n                    log.debug(\"{} from other classloader {} is visible from {}, excluding to prevent isolated loading\",\n                            type.simpleName(), pluginKlass.getClassLoader(), source);\n                    continue;\n                }\n                result.add(pluginDesc(pluginKlass, versionFor(pluginImpl), type, source));\n            }\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Helper to evaluate a {@link ServiceLoader} operation while handling {@link LinkageError}s.\n     *\n     * @param type The plugin type which is being loaded\n     * @param function A function on a {@link ServiceLoader}'s {@link Iterator} which may throw {@link LinkageError}\n     * @return the return value of function\n     * @throws Error errors thrown by the passed-in function\n     * @param <U> Return value of the passed-in function\n     */\n    private <U> U handleLinkageError(PluginType type, PluginSource source, Supplier<U> function) {\n        // It's difficult to know for sure if the iterator was able to advance past the first broken\n        // plugin class, or if it will continue to fail on that broken class for any subsequent calls\n        // to Iterator::hasNext or Iterator::next\n        // For reference, see https://bugs.openjdk.org/browse/JDK-8196182, which describes\n        // the behavior we are trying to mitigate with this logic as buggy, but indicates that a fix\n        // in the JDK standard library ServiceLoader implementation is unlikely to land\n        LinkageError lastError = null;\n        // Try a fixed maximum number of times in case the ServiceLoader cannot move past a faulty plugin,\n        // but the LinkageError varies between calls. This limit is chosen to be higher than the typical number\n        // of plugins in a single plugin location, and to limit the amount of log-spam on startup.\n        for (int i = 0; i < 100; i++) {\n            try {\n                return function.get();\n            } catch (LinkageError t) {\n                // As an optimization, hide subsequent error logs if two consecutive errors look similar.\n                // This reduces log-spam for iterators which cannot advance and rethrow the same exception.\n                if (lastError == null\n                        || !Objects.equals(lastError.getClass(), t.getClass())\n                        || !Objects.equals(lastError.getMessage(), t.getMessage())) {\n                    log.error(\"Failed to discover {} in {}{}\",\n                            type.simpleName(), source, reflectiveErrorDescription(t.getCause()), t);\n                }\n                lastError = t;\n            }\n        }\n        log.error(\"Received excessive ServiceLoader errors: assuming the runtime ServiceLoader implementation cannot \" +\n                        \"skip faulty implementations. Use a different JRE, or resolve LinkageErrors for plugins in {}\",\n                source, lastError);\n        throw lastError;\n    }\n\n    protected static <T> String versionFor(T pluginImpl) {\n        try {\n            if (pluginImpl instanceof Versioned) {\n                return ((Versioned) pluginImpl).version();\n            }\n        } catch (Throwable t) {\n            log.error(\"Failed to get plugin version for {}\", pluginImpl.getClass(), t);\n        }\n        return PluginDesc.UNDEFINED_VERSION;\n    }\n\n    protected static String reflectiveErrorDescription(Throwable t) {\n        if (t instanceof NoSuchMethodException) {\n            return \": Plugin class must have a no-args constructor, and cannot be a non-static inner class\";\n        } else if (t instanceof SecurityException) {\n            return \": Security settings must allow reflective instantiation of plugin classes\";\n        } else if (t instanceof IllegalAccessException) {\n            return \": Plugin class default constructor must be public\";\n        } else if (t instanceof ExceptionInInitializerError) {\n            return \": Failed to statically initialize plugin class\";\n        } else if (t instanceof InvocationTargetException) {\n            return \": Failed to invoke plugin constructor\";\n        } else if (t instanceof LinkageError) {\n            return \": Plugin class has a dependency which is missing or invalid\";\n        } else {\n            return \"\";\n        }\n    }\n\n    protected LoaderSwap withClassLoader(ClassLoader loader) {\n        ClassLoader savedLoader = Plugins.compareAndSwapLoaders(loader);\n        try {\n            return new LoaderSwap(savedLoader);\n        } catch (Throwable t) {\n            Plugins.compareAndSwapLoaders(savedLoader);\n            throw t;\n        }\n    }\n}\n","numLines":234,"startLine":1,"totalLines":234}}}

plugin/extension loading system for Connect, Converter, and HeaderConverter plugins using classloader isolation and reflection-based discovery.\\n\\n## Core Plugin Classloading System\\n\\nThe foundation consists of custom classloaders:\\n- **PluginClassLoader** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginClassLoader.java) extends URLClassLoader and implements child-first classloading. It loads plugin classes in isolation using PluginUtils.shouldLoadInIsolation() to determine which classes to isolate. Thread-safe with support for parallel loading.\\n- **DelegatingClassLoader** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/DelegatingClassLoader.java) coordinates multiple PluginClassLoaders, delegating to child loaders first before delegating to parent. Manages plugin class loading with version range support via VersionRange.\\n- **ClassLoaderFactory** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ClassLoaderFactory.java) creates isolated classloaders\\n- **LoaderSwap** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/LoaderSwap.java) provides context management for temporarily swapping thread context classloaders\\n\\n## Plugin Discovery via Reflection and ServiceLoader\\n\\nPlugin discovery uses two complementary strategies implemented in PluginScanner subclasses:\\n\\n**ReflectionScanner** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ReflectionScanner.java) - Legacy approach:\\n- Uses ClassGraph library to scan classpath for implementations\\n- Discovers subclasses/implementers of SinkConnector, SourceConnector, Converter, HeaderConverter, Transformation, and Predicate\\n- Instantiates each plugin to validate it can be constructed and get version info\\n- Requires no manifest files but slower performance\\n\\n**ServiceLoaderScanner** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ServiceLoaderScanner.java) - Modern approach:\\n- Uses Java ServiceLoader mechanism with META-INF/services/ manifests\\n- Faster and more efficient than reflection scanning\\n- Follows standard plugin discovery pattern\\n\\n**PluginScanner** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginScanner.java) is the abstract base class providing:\\n- discoverPlugins() entry point for scanning multiple PluginSource instances\\n- getServiceLoaderPluginDesc() for ServiceLoader-based discovery\\n- Error handling for LinkageError and ServiceConfigurationError\\n- Version detection via Versioned interface\\n\\n## Plugin Descriptor and Registry\\n\\n- **PluginDesc** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginDesc.java) holds metadata: class, version (via DefaultArtifactVersion), type, and classloader\\n- **PluginType** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginType.java) enum categorizes plugins: SOURCE, SINK, CONVERTER, HEADER_CONVERTER, TRANSFORMATION, PREDICATE, CONFIGPROVIDER, REST_EXTENSION, CONNECTOR_CLIENT_CONFIG_OVERRIDE_POLICY\\n- **PluginScanResult** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginScanResult.java) aggregates discovered plugins by type\\n- **PluginSource** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginSource.java) represents a source of plugins (JAR locations)\\n\\n## Interface-Based Dependency Injection\\n\\nThe plugin system uses interface-based dependency injection:\\n\\n1. **Configurable** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/Configurable.java) - Mix-in interface for classes instantiated by reflection needing configuration. Provides configure(Map<String, ?> configs) method.\\n\\n2. **Converter** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/Converter.java) - Plugin interface for data format conversion. Implementations are discovered and instantiated, then configured via configure(Map<String, ?> configs, boolean isKey).\\n\\n3. **HeaderConverter** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/HeaderConverter.java) - Extends Configurable. Plugin interface for header conversion. Discovered and instantiated with configure(Map<String, ?> configs).\\n\\n4. **Connector** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/connector/Connector.java) - Base class for SourceConnector and SinkConnector. Implements Versioned interface. Implements dependency injection via initialize(ConnectorContext ctx) and configure(Map<String, String> props).\\n\\n5. **Versioned** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/components/Versioned.java) - Interface for versioned components. Creates configured Converter instances using newVersionedPlugin()\\n- newHeaderConverter(AbstractConfig, String propertyName, ClassLoaderUsage) - Creates configured HeaderConverter instances\\n- newPlugin(Class<T>) - Generic factory instantiating plugins via Utils.newInstance() with appropriate thread context classloader\\n- Dependency injection happens via configure() method calls after instantiation\\n- Thread-safe with LoaderSwap context managers\\n\\n## Plugin Discovery Modes\\n\\n**PluginDiscoveryMode** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginDiscoveryMode.java) enum controls discovery strategy:\\n- SERVICE_LOAD: Modern ServiceLoader-only approach\\n- ONLY_SCAN: Legacy reflection-only approach  \\n- HYBRID_WARN: Both approaches with warnings\\n- HYBRID_FAIL: Both approaches with errors on differences\\n\\n## Utility Functions\\n\\n**PluginUtils** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginUtils.java) provides:\\n- shouldLoadInIsolation(String className) -
